{"nick":"Sorella","message":"TexMax: usually, you'll require each module where you need to use it, that way you're being explicit about what dependencies your module has to work. However, in some cases, it might be better to not fix the dependency to a particular implementation. For example, if you don't want to tie your module to Node's file system (maybe you want to use that module","date":"2015-09-21T13:23:46.595Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"Sorella","message":"for both Node and the Browser), then you can make your module accept the filesystem module as a parameter, rather than require a particular implementation of it.
